Each event must be marked as handled\\n59: \\t// with a call to Done() which marks the key processed. No new events for this key\\n60: \\t// will be emitted before Done() is called.\\n61: \\t//\\n62: \\t// A missing Done() will lead to an eventual panic (via finalizer on Event[T]).\\n63: \\t// Panic on this situation is needed as otherwise no new events would be emitted\\n64: \\t// and thus this needs to be enforced.\\n65: \\t//\\n66: \\t// A stream of Upsert events are emitted first to replay the current state of the\\n67: \\t// store after which incremental upserts and deletes follow until the underlying\\n68: \\t// store is synchronized after which a Sync event is emitted and further incremental\\n69: \\t// updates:\\n70: \\t//\\n71: \\t//\\t(start observing), Upsert, Upsert, Upsert, (done replaying store contents), Upsert, Upsert,\\n72: \\t//\\t  (store synchronized with API server), Sync, Upsert, Delete, Upsert, ...\\n73: \\t//\\n74: \\t// The emitting of the Sync event does not depend on whether or not Upsert events have\\n75: \\t// all been marked Done() without an error. The sync event solely signals that the underlying\\n76: \\t// store has synchronized and that Upsert events for objects in a synchronized store have been\\n77: \\t// sent to the observer.\\n78: \\t//\\n79: \\t// When Done() is called with non-nil error the error handler is invoked, which\\n80: \\t// can ignore, requeue the event (by key) or close the channel. The default error handler\\n81: \\t// will requeue.\\n82: \\t//\\n83: \\t// If an Upsert is retried and the object has been deleted, a Delete event will be emitted instead.\\n84: \\t// Conversely if a Delete event is retried and the object has been recreated with the same key,\\n85: \\t// an Upsert will be emitted instead.\\n86: \\t//\\n87: \\t// If an objects is created and immediately deleted, then a slow observer may not observe this at\\n88: \\t// all. In all cases a Delete event is only emitted if the observer has seen an Upsert. Whether or\\n89: \\t// not it had been successfully handled (via Done(nil)) does not affect this property.\\n90: \\tEvents(ctx context.Context, opts ...EventsOpt) <-chan Event[T]\\n91: \\n92: \\t// Store retrieves the read-only store for the resource. Blocks until\\n93: \\t// the store has been synchronized or the context cancelled.\\n94: \\t// Returns a non-nil error if context is cancelled or the resource\\n95: \\t// has been stopped before store has synchronized.\\n96: \\tStore(context.Context) (Store[T], error)\\n97: }\\n98: \\n99: // New creates a new Resource[T]. \\t\\tonPodEvent(ev)\\n119: //\\t\\t   \\t}\\n120: //\\t\\t}\\n121: //\\t\\treturn e\\n122: //\\t}\\n123: //\\tfunc onPodEvent(event resource.Event[*slim_core.Pod]) {\\n124: //\\t\\tswitch event.Kind SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0\n// Copyright Authors of Cilium\n\npackage quota\n\nimport (\n\t\"context\"\n\t\"fmt\"\n\t\"sync\"\n\n\t\"github.com/sirupsen/logrus\"\n\n\tcilium_v2 \"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/k8s/apis/cilium.io/v2\"\n\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/k8s/resource\"\n\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/logging/logfields\"\n)\n\nvar (\n\tlog = logrus.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.LogSubsys: \"policy-quota\",\n\t})\n)\n\n// PolicyQuotaController manages per-namespace limits on the number of\n// CiliumNetworkPolicy resources.\ntype PolicyQuotaController struct {\n\tlog                  logrus.FieldLogger\n\tcnpResource          resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy]\n\tpolicyQuotaResource  resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumPolicyQuota]\n\tmaxPerNamespace      int\n\tnamespacePolicyCounts sync.Map // map[string]int - namespace to policy count\n\tmu                   sync.RWMutex\n}\n\n// NewPolicyQuotaController creates a new PolicyQuotaController.\nfunc NewPolicyQuotaController(\n\tlogger logrus.FieldLogger,\n\tcnpResource resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy],\n\tpolicyQuotaResource resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumPolicyQuota],\n\tmaxPerNamespace int,\n) *PolicyQuotaController {\n\treturn &PolicyQuotaController{\n\t\tlog:                 logger,\n\t\tcnpResource:         cnpResource,\n\t\tpolicyQuotaResource: policyQuotaResource,\n\t\tmaxPerNamespace:     maxPerNamespace,\n\t}\n}\n\n// Run starts the controller loop that watches CiliumNetworkPolicy resources\n// and tracks policy counts per namespace.\nfunc (pc *PolicyQuotaController) Run(ctx context.Context) {\n\tpc.log.Info(\"Starting PolicyQuotaController\")\n\n\t// Watch both CNP and PolicyQuota resources\n\tcnpEvents := pc.cnpResource.Events(ctx)\n\tquotaEvents := pc.policyQuotaResource.Events(ctx)\n\n\tfor {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n\t\t\tpc.log.Info(\"Stopping PolicyQuotaController\")\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\tcase event, ok := <-cnpEvents:\n\t\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\t\tcnpEvents = nil\n\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tpc.handleCNPEvent(event)\n\t\tcase event, ok := <-quotaEvents:\n\t\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\t\tquotaEvents = nil\n\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tpc.handleQuotaEvent(event)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Exit if both channels are closed\n\t\tif cnpEvents == nil && quotaEvents == nil {\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// handleCNPEvent processes events for CiliumNetworkPolicy resources.\nfunc (pc *PolicyQuotaController) handleCNPEvent(event resource.Event[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy]) {\n\tdefer event.Done(nil)\n\n\tif event.Kind == resource.Sync {\n\t\tpc.log.Debug(\"CNP resources synced\")\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tcnp := event.Object\n\tnamespace := cnp.GetNamespace()\n\n\tswitch event.Kind {\n\tcase resource.Upsert:\n\t\t// Increment policy count for namespace\n\t\tpc.incrementNamespaceCount(namespace)\n\tcase resource.Delete:\n\t\t// Decrement policy count for namespace\n\t\tpc.decrementNamespaceCount(namespace)\n\t}\n}\n\n// handleQuotaEvent processes events for CiliumPolicyQuota resources.\nfunc (pc *PolicyQuotaController) handleQuotaEvent(event resource.Event[*cilium_v2.CiliumPolicyQuota]) {\n\tdefer event.Done(nil)\n\n\tif event.Kind == resource.Sync {\n\t\tpc.log.Debug(\"PolicyQuota resources synced\")\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tquota := event.Object\n\tif quota == nil {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tpc.mu.Lock()\n\tif event.Kind == resource.Upsert {\n\t\t// Update max policies per namespace if quota is updated\n\t\tpc.maxPerNamespace = int(quota.Spec.MaxPoliciesPerNamespace)\n\t\tpc.log.WithField(\"maxPerNamespace\", pc.maxPerNamespace).\n\t\t\tDebug(\"Updated maximum policies per namespace\")\n\t}\n\tpc.mu.Unlock()\n}\n\n// CheckQuota checks if adding a new policy would exceed the quota for the given namespace.\nfunc (pc *PolicyQuotaController) CheckQuota(namespace string) error {\n\tpc.mu.RLock()\n\tdefer pc.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\tcount, _ := pc.namespacePolicyCounts.LoadOrStore(namespace, 0)\n\tcurrentCount := count.(int)\n\n\tif currentCount >= pc.maxPerNamespace {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"policy quota
